# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes API Deprecation Policy Enforcement

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that enforce the API deprecation policy: the deprecated API version warning injection, the removal version validation, and the minimum supported API version checks in the API server.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the compliance domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [

  ],

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

## Summary

I've identified all the key Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that enforce the Kubernetes API deprecation policy:

### **Core Files:**

1. **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/deprecation/deprecation.go`** - The foundational file implementing deprecation detection with:
   - `IsDeprecated()` - Checks if API version is deprecated
   - `RemovedRelease()` - Gets the version when API will be removed
   - `WarningMessage()` - Generates human-readable deprecation warnings
   - Three interfaces for API lifecycle: `apiLifecycleDeprecated`, `apiLifecycleRemoved`, `apiLifecycleReplacement`

2. **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/warning/warning.go`** - Injects deprecation warnings into HTTP response headers via `AddWarningsHandler()`

3. **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/installer.go`** - Integrates deprecation checks into API server routing, calling deprecation functions and applying warnings to all HTTP handlers

4. **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/metrics/metrics.go`** - Records metrics for deprecated API requests and adds audit annotations:
   - `deprecatedAnnotationKey` ("k8s.io/deprecated")
   - `removedReleaseAnnotationKey` ("k8s.io/removed-release")

5. **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go`** - Handles CRD version deprecation with `defaultDeprecationWarning()`

6. **Code generation files** (`prerelease-lifecycle-gen/`) - Auto-generates APILifecycleDeprecated(), APILifecycleRemoved(), and APILifecycleReplacement() methods

Methods\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/code-generator/cmd/prerelease-lifecycle-gen/main.go** and **status.go** (lines 483-491) implement the code generator that:\\n- Processes `+k8s:prerelease-lifecycle-gen:deprecated=<major>.<minor>` tags on types\\n- Processes `+k8s:prerelease-lifecycle-gen:removed=<major>.<minor>` tags on types\\n- Processes types\\n- Auto-generated methods produce zz_generated.prerelease-lifecycle.go files across the codebase\\n\\n## Enforcement Workflow\\n\\n1. API types define lifecycle information through build tags in their type definitions\\n2. Code generator creates APILifecycleDeprecated(), APILifecycleRemoved(), and APILifecycleReplacement() methods\\n3. When the API server starts, installer.go registers endpoints and checks deprecation status\\n4. For each request to a deprecated API:\\n   - deprecation.IsDeprecated() returns true\\n   - deprecation.RemovedRelease() provides removal version\\n   - deprecation.WarningMessage() generates user-facing warning\\n   - AddWarningsHandler() injects warning into HTTP response headers\\n   - MonitorRequest() records metrics and audit annotations\\n5. Clients receive warnings in HTTP headers and administrators see metrics/audit logs\\n\\nThis multi-layer enforcement ensures deprecated APIs are clearly marked in responses, tracked in metrics, and audited, allowing operators to identify and migrate away from deprecated APIs before removal.\"\n}\n",
